let lateral_surface_area r h =
  let r2 = r * r in
  let h2 = h * h in
  let r2h2 = r2 * h2 in

 (* Write a function to find the lateral surface area of a cylinder. *)
let lateral_surface_area r h =
  let r2 = r * r in
  let h2 = h * h in
  let r2h2 = r2 * h2 in

let lateral_surface_area r h =
  let r2 = r * r in
  let h2 = h * h in
  let r2h2 = r2 * h2 in

let lateral_surface_area r h =
  let r2 = r * r in
  let h2 = h * h in
  let r2h2 = r2 * h2 in
